<div id="review_2270746390" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2270746390" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2270746390?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=2018-reads">2018-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=fae">fae</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2270746390" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16364538891707564444"><b>Brace yourselves, folks, we're jumping on the hype wagon!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1516826905ra/24904059.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If I cannot be better than them, I will become so much worse.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><b>
  <u>First Stop: Elfhame</u>
</b><br/>With all the raving reviews about <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26032825.The_Cruel_Prince__The_Folk_of_the_Air___1_' title='The Cruel Prince (The Folk of the Air, #1) by Holly Black' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Cruel Prince</a>, how could little ol' Katerina resist? The Hype (yes, Hype with a capital H because it's a being of its own that swallows the innocent and the weak) was a siren, luring me to dive into its dark waters, and, thankfully, I was not eaten alive. With <b>a successful blend of modern world and faerie </b></span>
  <span id="freeText16364538891707564444" style="display:none"><b>Brace yourselves, folks, we're jumping on the hype wagon!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1516826905ra/24904059.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If I cannot be better than them, I will become so much worse.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <u>First Stop: Elfhame</u>
</b><br>With all the raving reviews about <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26032825.The_Cruel_Prince__The_Folk_of_the_Air___1_" title="The Cruel Prince (The Folk of the Air, #1) by Holly Black" rel="nofollow noopener">The Cruel Prince</a>, how could little ol' Katerina resist? The Hype (yes, Hype with a capital H because it's a being of its own that swallows the innocent and the weak) was a siren, luring me to dive into its dark waters, and, thankfully, I was not eaten alive. With <b>a successful blend of modern world and faerie lore</b>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/25422.Holly_Black" title="Holly Black" rel="nofollow noopener">Holly Black</a> created <b>a dangerous and mesmerizing tale</b>, a gripping saga focused on <b>intrigue, schemes and backstabbings</b>. Jude was seven years old when a cruel fae showed up on her doorstep, murdering her parents and taking her and her sisters to the realm of the Immortals, a realm so <b>beautiful</b> and <b>imposing</b> that hid how <b>rotten</b> and <b>tainted</b> it was on the inside. Despite her best efforts, Jude was always humiliated and taunted, a worm daring to live and train among their perfect kin. And her greatest tormentor? Prince Cardan and his band of <s>merry</s> evil <s>men</s> minions. With the coronation of the next king approaching, Jude found her opportunity to shine, to grab a place for herself and hold it with her bleeding hands. But with plots set into motion, and disorienting deceptions, maybe finding her place means giving up the little humanity that's still left in her.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Because you're like a story that hasn't happened yet. Because I want to see what you will do. I want to be part of the unfolding of the tale.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <u>Next stop: Lake of Backstabbing</u>
</b><br>People who compare <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26032825.The_Cruel_Prince__The_Folk_of_the_Air___1_" title="The Cruel Prince (The Folk of the Air, #1) by Holly Black" rel="nofollow noopener">The Cruel Prince</a> to Game of Thrones are not exaggerating. <b>The conspiracies, the hidden agendas, and the masterful way they unfold</b> manage to keep you at the edge of your seat thoughout the story, you sweat and sweat and wonder who has the upper hand and who is going to perish, whose blood is going to spill, who is the good guy and who the villain (well, in all honesty all of them are the villains but a girl can hope, right?), and you can't help but feel a rush of adrenaline each time those horrible creatures <b>plot</b> and <b>stab</b> and <b>spy</b> and then plot some more. And when all this plotting and stabbing and spying takes place in idyllic landscapes, manors and balls, you can understand why I'm such a goner.<br><br><b>
  <u>Next stop: Temple of Hate</u>
</b><br>A curious thing happened with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26032825.The_Cruel_Prince__The_Folk_of_the_Air___1_" title="The Cruel Prince (The Folk of the Air, #1) by Holly Black" rel="nofollow noopener">The Cruel Prince</a>; <b>I didn't like the main characters.</b> At all. Was I <b>fascinated</b>? Of course, they were <b>beautiful and monstrous</b>, and that combination sparked a flare of curiosity to see how their stories will play out, but come on, they're horrible! (expect Vivi, you go girl!)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1511664763ra/24534646.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Beneath her frail mortal body and her too-short lifespan, Jude was a hungry, ruthless beast craving power, scheming, betraying, and wanting with a fiery need to become one the creatures that tortured her and rejected her. I was rooting for her to an extent, if only to teach those awful fae that expendable humans can outmaneuver them, but she really needs to calm down, this hunger consumed her thoughts and didn't leave place for other, more pleasant sentiments. <s>Don't get me started on her parade of stupid decisions</s>. And Cardan was not better. Fine YES I had a tiny crush on him (thumbs up for dark jerks who hide their pain), but that doesn't erase the fact that he's cruel, irresponsible and petty, a true bully. Madoc, Locke, Dain, Taryn, they were hideous, but let me tell you this, that is not a bad thing. Sure, I didn't particularly connect with them, but this detachment liberated me from the usual fear for their lives, or sorrow for their misfortunes, only the occassional anger and disgust. <b>I was invested in their story and <i>not</i> in them</b>, but somehow this magnified the reading experience! I was there for the bumpy ride, for the malice and the power bid, I sank my teeth into their rotten fruit and was bewitched by their depravity. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There's always something left to lose.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <u>Terminal station: Vale of Fangirling</u>
</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26032825.The_Cruel_Prince__The_Folk_of_the_Air___1_" title="The Cruel Prince (The Folk of the Air, #1) by Holly Black" rel="nofollow noopener">The Cruel Prince</a> was a <b>beguiling, wicked tale of power, lust, secrets and magic</b>. The world <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/25422.Holly_Black" title="Holly Black" rel="nofollow noopener">Holly Black</a> painted, with her lush descriptions, the revels and the colourful creatures that came straight out of a storybook is a place worth visiting, and cherishing. <b>Drunk on enchanted wine, exhausted from dancing in fancy dresses until my foot hurt, clammy from the swordfights but deliciously invigorated, I am all too eager to return to Elfhame and be a part of the High Court!</b><br><br><a href="http://booknest.eu/reviews/kat/1023-thecruelprince" rel="nofollow noopener">You can find this review and more on BookNest!</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16364538891707564444" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2240560654" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2240560654" />
    <a title="Kai" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41788524-kai"><img alt="Kai" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1573562141p2/41788524.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2240560654?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kai" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kai" href="/user/show/41788524-kai">Kai</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41788524-kai?shelf=finished-series">finished-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41788524-kai?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41788524-kai?shelf=2018">2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2240560654" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3761515395788969898"><i>“I have lied and I have betrayed and I have triumphed.”</i><br/><br/>Um yes, I totally gave in to the hype and for once I am glad.<br/><br/>After reading <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20958632.The_Darkest_Part_of_the_Forest' title='The Darkest Part of the Forest by Holly Black' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Darkest Part of the Forest</a>, I developed a sudden thirst for more faerie stories and more Holly Black. <i>The Cruel Prince</i> was like a gift from heaven. By the way, if you have only read one of these two books, you might be interested in checking out the other. You might recognise a few characters.<br/><br/>This book is like paradise for fans of young adult fantasy. Naturally, I</span>
  <span id="freeText3761515395788969898" style="display:none"><i>“I have lied and I have betrayed and I have triumphed.”</i><br /><br />Um yes, I totally gave in to the hype and for once I am glad.<br /><br />After reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20958632.The_Darkest_Part_of_the_Forest" title="The Darkest Part of the Forest by Holly Black" rel="nofollow noopener">The Darkest Part of the Forest</a>, I developed a sudden thirst for more faerie stories and more Holly Black. <i>The Cruel Prince</i> was like a gift from heaven. By the way, if you have only read one of these two books, you might be interested in checking out the other. You might recognise a few characters.<br /><br />This book is like paradise for fans of young adult fantasy. Naturally, I was captivated right from the start. I had no idea where the story was going to go. So many unexpected things were happening, and even though some of them were somewhat predictable, I was caught off guard several times. However, I cannot decide whether I think the plot was chaotic or refreshing. The events in this book could have gone in so many directions. And this book tipped the fine line between a complete mess and a good structure.<br />This might also be related to the main character. I could not get a good feeling for her, as in, her goals and motivations were clearly spelt out, but her voice did not match her actions. On one hand, Jude is this ruthless human with a backbone like a lion, and on the other hand, she is a typical young adult main character that could be interchanged with several other MCs from different novels. I could not make these two aspects fit in one person. I hope she grows into her skin and goes through strong character development in the sequels.<br /><br />Now, the hate-to-love trope is one that I love. It can be so much fun if it is well-written. However, I condemn volatile and unhealthy relationships in novels. That is not romance. It troubles me to see characters that hurt and treat one another in the most despicable ways develope a romantic relationship based on such feelings. This sends a wrong message to the readers. I cannot see such behaviour turned into a pairing and I seriously do not know how this relationship would ever work in the future. I hope Holly Black does not plan a happily ever after for the characters that I have in mind.<br /><br />Other than that, I am so looking forward to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26032887.The_Wicked_King__The_Folk_of_the_Air___2_" title="The Wicked King (The Folk of the Air, #2) by Holly Black" rel="nofollow noopener">The Wicked King</a>. <i>The Cruel Prince</i> was already wicked, thrilling, nerve-wracking and enchanted, and I must admit that I am a little scared to see what will happen next.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.instagram.com/fantasticbooksandwheretofindem/" rel="nofollow noopener">Find more of my books on Instagram</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="3761515395788969898" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2073418506" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2073418506" />
    <a title="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries"><img alt="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557144778p2/15335689.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2073418506?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" href="/user/show/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries">destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780316480208" href="/book/show/36511768-the-cruel-prince">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=fae">fae</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=owned-physical">owned-physical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2073418506" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer458139850418179347"><blockquote>#1 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2073418506' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Cruel Prince</a> ★★★★★<br/>#2 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2519986163' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Wicked King</a> ★★★★★<br/>#3 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2267451762' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Queen of Nothing</a> ???<br/> <br/><i>If I cannot be better than them, I will become so much worse.</i></blockquote><br/>It had been years since I’d picked up a Holly Black book, but I loved her writing as a kid, so I was a little bit apprehensive about re-entering her little fae world. Believe me when I say, though, that this book was everything I wanted it to be and so much more. Her writing is impeccable, the lore is woven seamlessly through the tale, the characters are lovab</span>
  <span id="freeText458139850418179347" style="display:none"><blockquote>#1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2073418506" rel="nofollow noopener">The Cruel Prince</a> ★★★★★<br />#2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2519986163" rel="nofollow noopener">The Wicked King</a> ★★★★★<br />#3 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2267451762" rel="nofollow noopener">The Queen of Nothing</a> ???<br /> <br /><i>If I cannot be better than them, I will become so much worse.</i></blockquote><br />It had been years since I’d picked up a Holly Black book, but I loved her writing as a kid, so I was a little bit apprehensive about re-entering her little fae world. Believe me when I say, though, that this book was everything I wanted it to be and so much more. Her writing is impeccable, the lore is woven seamlessly through the tale, the characters are lovable and disastrously grey (which is my favorite, forever), and I just wanted <b>
  <i>more.</i>
</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I promise you this” – I throw his own words back at him – “this is the least of what I can do.”</i>
</blockquote><br />→ <b>Jude</b> ←<br />I’m going to get this out of the way early: if you asked me what my favorite thing about this book was, I would probably take three years to decide between Holly’s writing voice itself… or this fantastically grey, authentic, <i>human</i> protagonist. She is angry, terrified, clever, and determined. I’ve heard many people say they thought she was annoying, and while I totally respect everyone’s opinions, I can’t see it – if anything, she just felt tremendously real to me.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Even if, by some miracle, I could be better than them, I will never be one of them.</i>
</blockquote><br />She has undergone incredible traumas, and continues to live through daily abuse – be it verbal or physical – yet, she manages to shove down her pain and fears for the most part. The fact that she was willing to admit to herself that she was secretly terrified, every moment of every day, made her a three-dimensional character that I could relate to. Despite her fears, she does everything she can to even the playing fields, which I found rather admirable.<br /><br />And then… that ending? I mean, I won’t spoil, but <i>damn.</i> Jude is more than willing to vilify herself to do what she thinks is best for the people she loves and hopes to protect, and it just made me love her even more than I already did.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>I am coming unraveled. I am coming undone.</i>
</blockquote><br />→ <b>Prince Cardan</b> ←<br />For all that I loved Jude’s moral greyness, Cardan’s left me feeling conflicted a lot of the time. I feel like I have a little bit of an unpopular opinion in that I wasn’t left swooning for the prince; unfortunately, a lot of his behaviors were borderline unforgivable for me.<br /><br />That said, I do understand that Cardan’s life has been far from easy, and a lot of his behaviors can be somewhat explained (though not justified) by his circumstances. And, I won’t lie, the shift in his attitude towards the end of the book is adorable and far more lovable than his entire existence in the first half of the book, so I still have high hopes that he’ll win me over in the sequel!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Despite myself, despite what he’d done and what he was, I came to love him. I do love him. It’s just not a comfortable kind of love.</i>
</blockquote><br />→ <b>family</b> ←<br />Reason #347 why Holly is such a fantastic author: she can make your feelings for a character shift so quickly in one direction or the other, with little to no warning, and Jude’s family is evidence of this from start to finish.<br /><br />•	<b>Madoc</b> – Jude’s “father figure”, who took away her parents only to take her in and raise her. He’s brutal, yet doting, and Jude’s feelings for him were a really interesting and realistic view of Stockholm syndrome, in which she constantly was reminded of the terrible things he had done for her, yet she couldn’t seem to stop herself from loving him and wanting to please him. The best part of this is that his character arc is written so flawlessly, <i>I fell for it, too.</i><br /><br />•	<b>Taryn</b> — her twin sister, who ranges from “meh” to downright infuriating and hate-worthy, depending on which scene you’re reading. (Mostly the latter.)<br /><br />•	<b>Vivienne</b> — she’s bisexual, rebellious, fun, caring, snarky, and one of my favorite characters in this book by far. I loved each chance that we got to spend time with her, and if there was ever a novella about her life with her cute little mortal girlfriend, I’d be so here for it.<br /><br />•	<b>Oriana</b> — the other half of Jude’s makeshift parenting duo, who strikes out as aloof and cold, but has a surprisingly love development process throughout the story that made me genuinely hope we see more of her in the future, as I think she could be a valuable ally for Jude in the coming trials.<br /><br />•	<b>Oak</b> — Oriana’s son, who is tiny, adorable, and wild. He’s the perfect portrayal of Fair Folk in that, despite how lovely and charming he can be, he has a vicious and mischievous streak in his bones that few fae are wholly exempt from.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i> “Plenty of mortals are better at plenty of stuff than the Folk. Why do you think we steal them away?”</i>
</blockquote><br />→ <b>fair folk</b> ←<br />One of the many things I enjoyed about this story is how many side characters there were, and how fleshed out most of them felt! My favorite side character was easily one of Jude’s fellow spies, Ghost, who takes it upon himself to spend immense amounts of time training her in how to sneak, steal, and kill. It’s not just that he mentors her, though – it’s that he respects her, and treats her as his equal throughout all of their interactions. So help me, if he does not get MAJOR screen time in the following books, <b>I WILL RIOT.</b><br /><br />Among other noteworthy characters were Locke, who is a complete raging asshole that I will never forgive in a million years ever, and the rest of Cardan’s posse, who were also, well… complete raging assholes that I will never forgive in a million years ever.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Faerie might be beautiful, but its beauty is like a golden stag’s carcass, crawling with maggots beneath his hide, ready to burst.</i>
</blockquote><br />→ <b>final thoughts</b> ←<br />All in all, while there were some aspects to the story that I didn’t love, I thought this was such a phenomenal story with a delightfully bizarre and varied cast of characters. I felt like I couldn’t get enough of the world that Holly Black wrote, and the idea of having to wait an entire year to see what happens next <i>physically pains me.</i> I highly recommend this book to anyone who enjoys stories of fair folk, political intrigue, backstabbing, love, family, and conniving schemes.<br /><br /><b>Content warning:</b> Let me emphasize that, when you see TWs for abuse, people are not joking – as someone who has been bullied and abused, parts of this book were actually incredibly difficult for me to swallow. If you are triggered by scenes of abuse and harassment, <i>please</i> practice self-care before, during, and after this read.<br /><br />Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7772979-jue" rel="nofollow noopener">Julie</a>! &lt;3</span>
  <a data-text-id="458139850418179347" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2239952302" />
    <a title="Nilufer Ozmekik" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/53701594-nilufer-ozmekik"><img alt="Nilufer Ozmekik" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559807601p2/53701594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2239952302?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nilufer Ozmekik" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nilufer Ozmekik" href="/user/show/53701594-nilufer-ozmekik">Nilufer Ozmekik</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2239952302" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3329447424105554869">I know you missed my star auctions… Here comes the new one! Let’s start with five billion! Did I hear five centillion! Are you out of your mind? I don’t think there are centillion stars on the universe! Well, red head lady slaps the bidder and gave this book FIVE CENTILLION STARS anyways! SOLD with an all exclusive trip to fae world ( limitless Chardonnay and tequila shots included)<br/><br/>Awwwwwwww I’m in love with this book! This is definitely a Tarantino story taken place at the Fae World and we have</span>
  <span id="freeText3329447424105554869" style="display:none">I know you missed my star auctions… Here comes the new one! Let’s start with five billion! Did I hear five centillion! Are you out of your mind? I don’t think there are centillion stars on the universe! Well, red head lady slaps the bidder and gave this book FIVE CENTILLION STARS anyways! SOLD with an all exclusive trip to fae world ( limitless Chardonnay and tequila shots included)<br /><br />Awwwwwwww I’m in love with this book! This is definitely a Tarantino story taken place at the Fae World and we have hero and heroine (half human half villanelle) who are cheater, liar, playing dirty and unfair and they’re match made in heaven. Normally I want to punch the people with those attributes but I’m drawn to them! I officially let them under my skin and now I’m singing “Hey Jude, don’t make it bad, take a sad song and make it better”<br /><br />This book is dark, entertaining, captivating and addictive. We have blood freezing, heart throbbing parts like GOT’s Red Wedding. But the worst part is it finishes so fast now my hands are shaking, legs are tapping, eyes are getting watery, I want it more and I have only one book left! I know the second one is even better. And as soon as I finish it, I’ll suffer from worse addiction withdrawals! There are 49 days for third book’s release ( shit October is 31 days so it is 50 days!!!! NOOOOOO!!!)<br /><br /> As a precaution my husband hid my kindle to prevent me starting the second book and locked me in our wine cellar (Ok, kidding, we’re not rich! He locked me at my bedroom with one case of Chardonnay, enough food for feeding an army -equal to my one course meal!-) but he forgot I had my spare key. Anyways, I stopped ironing his clothes and dishwashing as a punishment (Well, actually I never do them but don’t bother! I’m 2000’s Peggy Bundy with no children and better hairstyle!)<br /><br />So the things made me falling in love and craving 200 sequel books of this series are:<br /><br />-AMAZING CHARACTERIZATIONS:<br />Two misfit, outsider, black sheep of the families, did I tell you how much I love those wicked hero and ruthless heroine? : Jude and Cardan are my new Mickey and Mallory, Joker and Harley Quinn, Honey Bunny and Pumpkin.<br /><br /> Jude witnessed to her parents’ murder when she was a little girl and has been whisked away to live in Faerie world where she is neglected, bullied and unwanted from the others.<br /><br />And Cardan is youngest son of High King, tormented by his own brothers and grow up in a world of wildness, cruelness, savageness. He hasn’t been loved, pampered and only way to survive is acting like he didn’t care anything about power games and politics, staying drunk and making vicious and wicked circle of friends: Nicasia: power thirsty, Locke: drama king, Valerian: violence lover.<br />Less lovable and bringers of my slap urge: Locke and Taryn ( no spoilers but they are spineless human beings! Correction: woman being and faerie being)<br /><br />-CLIFFHANGER: I was expecting something surprising will come out and my spider senses didn’t surprise me (I climb to the walls to celebrate it)<br /><br />-FAST PACING, BLOODY ACTION PARTS, MANIPULATIONS, MIND AND POWER GAMES: I wish Holly Black took the seat of the last season of GOT and gave the bloody, violent and satisfying ending we deserved. At least she didn’t write something about a raven king, right? <br /><br />-LOVE STORY: Those characters are in love with power and they don’t know what it means to love somebody but they’re hopelessly drawn each other. This is Shakespearean kind of tragic story and I can feel it doesn’t have a proper HEA! But this obsessive, uncontrollable attraction of dark hero and heroine put a big, widen Joker smile on my face. It’s hot as hell!<br /><br />So 50 days to 3rd book and I’ll wait at least two weeks for the second book. ( It’s Catch 22 because reading and waiting are equally painful! I wish I could be patient enough till all the books release and I can devour them one by one) As a summary: My vote for Best Fantasy this year is obvious! This is also gotten its place at my all-time favorite books list!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3329447424105554869" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3241095826?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="She-who-must-not-be-named " class="user" itemprop="url" name="She-who-must-not-be-named " href="/user/show/106473614-she-who-must-not-be-named">She-who-must-not-be-named </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/106473614-she-who-must-not-be-named?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/106473614-she-who-must-not-be-named?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3241095826" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7941456756736138485">A story about three sisters and a conflict between Jude and Prince Cardan, this book focuses on the ruthlessness of fey and does, in no way downplay their ferocity. The dialogues and narrative are intriguing and the stunning betrayal in the end that changes everything in Faerie is worth mentioning.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('p3/YkCPvypPHUc1vbruI4a/rAYhp3IxCWdG/42aPWGBb2gK4ERgT5xF5E/PnI9qcFb3/vMnvF+zZ93kahWqpHw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('PqmmIUkeJuBhWhVNQ4uk+Ld4MXbiISwQy0TFN5IusGHCDHwJe+n/lLdyy9HKE/aFDS7PQkISt75LYgPOcctBHg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer17038619188154989118">Holly Black is the #1 New York Times bestselling author of over thirty fantasy novels for kids and teens. She has been a finalist for an Eisner Award and the Lodestar Award, and the recipient of the Mythopoeic Award, a Nebula, and a Newbery Honor. Her books have been translated into 32 languages worldwide and adapted for film. She currently lives in New England with her husband and son in a house </span>
  <span id="freeText17038619188154989118" style="display:none">Holly Black is the #1 New York Times bestselling author of over thirty fantasy novels for kids and teens. She has been a finalist for an Eisner Award and the Lodestar Award, and the recipient of the Mythopoeic Award, a Nebula, and a Newbery Honor. Her books have been translated into 32 languages worldwide and adapted for film. She currently lives in New England with her husband and son in a house with a secret library.</span>
